    display: inline;

  textarea, select, input {

  }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





When dragging a new tab the |GetDisplayNearestWindow| is holding drag_source_window_. Since in the first attempt detaching tab |GetDisplayNearestWindow| didn't get notify if the drag_source_window_ has been released then the second attempt join/merge into browser cause UaF.



<span class="line"><!---->When dragging a new tab the |GetDisplayNearestWindow| is holding drag_source_window_. Since in the first attempt detaching tab |GetDisplayNearestWindow| didn't get notify if the drag_source_window_ has been released then the second attempt join/merge into browser cause UaF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/exo/extended_drag_source.cc;drc=b0092c498210587441a9fcc2ff92f45acf54c632;l=362



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/exo/extended_drag_source.cc;drc=b0092c498210587441a9fcc2ff92f45acf54c632;l=362"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/exo/extended_drag_source.cc;drc=b0092c498210587441a9fcc2ff92f45acf54c632;l=362<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 104.0.5090.0 + Dev



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 104.0.5090.0 + Dev<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Linux-ChromeOS



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Linux-ChromeOS<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





(1) Open new browser and add one NTP.



<span class="line"><!---->(1) Open new browser and add one NTP.<!----></span>



<br>





(2) Detach one tab then merge the tab.



<span class="line"><!---->(2) Detach one tab then merge the tab.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

Date: Thu Jun 09 07:31:54 2022



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Thu Jun 09 07:31:54 2022<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[lacros] Fix use-after-free when merging/splitting browser tab.



<span class="line"><!---->[lacros] Fix use-after-free when merging/splitting browser tab.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When merging and splitting a browser tab from a single-tab window into another browser window, there's a race condition between when exo destroys the drag source window and when the dragged window is being shown. The dragged window uses the drag source window to determine its initial bounds on the screen, but when the drag source window has already been freed, it accesses freed memory, causing the use-after-free memory violation.



<span class="line"><!---->When merging and splitting a browser tab from a single-tab window into another browser window, there's a race condition between when exo destroys the drag source window and when the dragged window is being shown. The dragged window uses the drag source window to determine its initial bounds on the screen, but when the drag source window has already been freed, it accesses freed memory, causing the use-after-free memory violation.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The fix makes the ExtendedDragSource instance observe the drag source window to detect when it has been destroyed and falls back to a best guess for where to show the dragged window.



<span class="line"><!---->The fix makes the ExtendedDragSource instance observe the drag source window to detect when it has been destroyed and falls back to a best guess for where to show the dragged window.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Bug: 1330125



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1330125" title="Security: heap-after-free on components/exo/extended_drag_source.cc (Lacros)"><!---->Bug: 1330125<!----></a>



<br>

Please consult with any Chrome security contact (

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

Thanks for the rewards. I was hoping the reward was similar to another browser crash or remote attack from the browser, and I was shocked by the achievement rewards. Unfortunately, the achievement reward seems lower than usual remote exploit from the browser, the whole browser crashes, and Heap UaF too. I knew this issue could perform from a remote. My mistake didn't provide HTML or plugins, but since this UaF issue can be triggered with a simple movement/poc, I consider not providing that ( crafted html or plugin ) stuff.

<span class="line"><!----> are older bugs and received VRP reward decisions over a year ago - in April of 2021; since that time we have updated our policies around rewards for mitigated bugs. <br>



<br>





"We have recently updated the page to include clarifying information to help answer some of the questions you have asked us about particular reward decisions. 



<span class="line"><!---->"We have recently updated the page to include clarifying information to help answer some of the questions you have asked us about particular reward decisions. <!----></span>



<br>





There is a recent trend of reports away from issues triggered by remote content to issues that are strongly or solely dependent on user interaction. While we appreciate your efforts to discover and report these bugs, these issues are not as impactful or exploitable as those that demonstrate exploitability through remote content. 



<span class="line"><!---->There is a recent trend of reports away from issues triggered by remote content to issues that are strongly or solely dependent on user interaction. While we appreciate your efforts to discover and report these bugs, these issues are not as impactful or exploitable as those that demonstrate exploitability through remote content. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To reduce ambiguity and to provide more clarification, we have updated our Rewards section on our Rules page:



<span class="line"><!---->To reduce ambiguity and to provide more clarification, we have updated our Rewards section on our Rules page:<!----></span>



<br>





The amounts listed are for good quality reports that don't require complex or unlikely user interaction. Reports of issues that rely heavily or solely on user interaction, instead of being triggered by remote content, will generally receive significantly reduced rewards. Less convincing or more constrained bug submissions will likely qualify for reduced reward amounts, as chosen at the discretion of the reward panel.



<span class="line"><!---->The amounts listed are for good quality reports that don't require complex or unlikely user interaction. Reports of issues that rely heavily or solely on user interaction, instead of being triggered by remote content, will generally receive significantly reduced rewards. Less convincing or more constrained bug submissions will likely qualify for reduced reward amounts, as chosen at the discretion of the reward panel.<!----></span>



<br>





Reports of issues that involve implausible interaction, interactions a user would not be realistically convinced to perform, may not be rewarded. " 



<span class="line"><!---->Reports of issues that involve implausible interaction, interactions a user would not be realistically convinced to perform, may not be rewarded. " <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The same bugs you link would be receiving reduced rewards if they were reported now/since that policy change. 



<span class="line"><!---->The same bugs you link would be receiving reduced rewards if they were reported now/since that policy change. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I hope this helps provide some context. 



<span class="line"><!---->I hope this helps provide some context. <!----></span>
